LightNode for a couple of months now, and overall, I'm pretty satisfied. One of the main reasons I chose them was because they offer VPS locations in Dhaka, which is extremely rare among global providers. As someone based in Bangladesh, that local option really makes a difference in terms of latency and speed.Setting up the VPS was very fast—just a couple of minutes—and the control panel is clean and easy to navigate. Their pay-as-you-go (hourly billing) is also super useful when you’re running temporary projects or testing different setups.Performance-wise, the server has been stable. I use it mainly for hosting small websites and running scripts, and it’s handled everything smoothly so far. The SSD storage and NVMe speed are noticeable when working with larger files.The only downside I've experienced is the customer support. They’re not very responsive. couple of months now, and overall, I&#x27;m pretty satisfied. One of the main reasons I chose them was because they offer VPS locations in Dhaka, which is extremely rare among global providers. As someone based in Bangladesh, that local option really makes a difference in terms of latency and speed.<br/><br/>Setting up the VPS was very fast—just a couple of minutes—and the control panel is clean and easy to navigate. Their pay-as-you-go (hourly billing) is also super useful when you’re running temporary projects or testing different setups.<br/><br/>Performance-wise, the server has been stable. I use it mainly for hosting small websites and running scripts, and it’s handled everything smoothly so far. The SSD storage and NVMe speed are noticeable when working with larger files.<br/><br/>The only downside I&#x27;ve experienced is the customer support. They’re not very responsive. It usually takes a while to get a reply, and the answers can feel generic. Also, the network speed is capped at 100 Mbps, which is okay for many tasks but might be a limitation for heavy traffic or media-heavy apps.<br/><br/>Overall, LightNode is a great choice if you need VPS in specific regions like Dhaka, and you want flexible billing and fast deployment.
